abstract class TemplateEngine2  {
  void execute(int separator, int text, int templateds)
  {
    int C0 = 0;
    int C1 = 0;
    int C2 = 0;
    int D0 = 0;
    int D0p = 0;
    int D1 = 0;
    int D1p = 0;
    int D2 = 0;
    int D2p = 0;
    int BOOLEAN_SEPARATOR = 10;
    int R = 0;
    int temporaryText = 0;
    int lastIndexOfText = 0;
    lessPreciseBound((R < (((((((((((8 * text) * templateds) + ((8 * separator) * templateds)) + ((8 * separator) * text)) + ((8 * text) * text)) + ((8 * separator) * separator)) + ((8 * templateds) * templateds)) + (8 * text)) + (8 * templateds)) + (8 * separator)) + 8)) || (R == (((((((((((8 * text) * templateds) + ((8 * separator) * templateds)) + ((8 * separator) * text)) + ((8 * text) * text)) + ((8 * separator) * separator)) + ((8 * templateds) * templateds)) + (8 * text)) + (8 * templateds)) + (8 * separator)) + 8)));
    mostPreciseBound((R < ((text * templateds) + (separator * templateds))) || (R == ((text * templateds) + (separator * templateds))));
    if ((((text < 1) || (text == 1)) || ((templateds < 0) || (templateds == 0))) || ((separator < 0) || (separator == 0)))
    {
      return;
    }
    else
    {
      ;
    }
    int chunk = 0;
    int i = 0;
    while (i < templateds)
    {
      int j = 0;
      {
        temporaryText = ndInt2(lastIndexOfText, text);
        chunk = temporaryText - lastIndexOfText;
        lastIndexOfText = temporaryText;
      }
      D0p = D0; D0 = 0; C0 = C0 + 1;D0 = D0 + chunk;
      R = R + chunk;

        {

          lastIndexOfText = temporaryText;

abstract class TemplateEngineMultiTrace  {
  void execute(int text, int choice)
  {
    int C0 = 0;
    int C1 = 0;
    int D0 = 0;
    int D0p = 0;
    int D1 = 0;
    int D1p = 0;
    int BOOLEAN_SEPARATOR = 10;
    int R = 0;
    int temporaryText = 0;
    int lastIndexOfText = 0;
    lessPreciseBound((R < ((8 * text) + 8)) || (R == ((8 * text) + 8)));
    mostPreciseBound((R < text) || (R == text));
    if ((text < 1) || (text == 1))
    {
      return;
    }
    else
    {
      ;
    }
    int chunk = 0;
    if (!((choice < 10)) && !((choice == 10)))
    {
      int i = 0;
      while (i < text)
      {
        {
          temporaryText = ndInt2(lastIndexOfText, text);
          chunk = temporaryText - lastIndexOfText;
          lastIndexOfText = temporaryText;
        }
        D1p = D1; D1 = 0; C1 = C1 + 1;D1 = D1 + chunk;
        R = R + chunk;
        i = i + 1;
      }
    }
    else
    {
      int j = 0;
      while (j < text)
      {
        {
          temporaryText = ndInt2(lastIndexOfText, text);
          chunk = temporaryText - lastIndexOfText;
          lastIndexOfText = temporaryText;
        }
        D0p = D0; D0 = 0; C0 = C0 + 1;D0 = D0 + chunk;
        R = R + chunk;
        j = j + 1;
      }
    }
  }
  // Declare these methods such that these generated code can be parsed
  // Keep in sync with brbo2

  public abstract int ndInt2(int lower, int upper);
  public abstract boolean ndBool();
  public abstract void assume(boolean expression);

  public abstract void lessPreciseBound(boolean assertion);

abstract class TemplateEngineSimplifiedVariant  {
  void execute(int text)
  {
    int C0 = 0;
    int C1 = 0;
    int D0 = 0;
    int D0p = 0;
    int D1 = 0;
    int D1p = 0;
    int BOOLEAN_SEPARATOR = 10;
    int R = 0;
    int temporaryText = 0;
    int lastIndexOfText = 0;
    lessPreciseBound((R < (((8 * text) + (text * 8)) + 8)) || (R == (((8 * text) + (text * 8)) + 8)));
    mostPreciseBound((R < (text + text)) || (R == (text + text)));
    if ((text < 1) || (text == 1))
    {
      return;
    }
    else
    {
      ;
    }
    int chunk = 0;
    int i = 0;
    while (i < text)
    {
      {
        temporaryText = ndInt2(lastIndexOfText, text);
        chunk = temporaryText - lastIndexOfText;
        lastIndexOfText = temporaryText;
      }
      D1p = D1; D1 = 0; C1 = C1 + 1;D1 = D1 + chunk;
      R = R + chunk;
      D0p = D0; D0 = 0; C0 = C0 + 1;D0 = D0 + 1;
      R = R + 1;
      i = i + 1;
    }
  }

  void execute(int pattern, int stopIndex)
  {
    int C0 = 0;
    int D0 = 0;
    int D0p = 0;
    int BOOLEAN_SEPARATOR = 10;
    int R = 0;
    int temporaryStopIndex = 0;
    int lastIndexOfStopIndex = 0;
    lessPreciseBound((R < ((8 * pattern) + 8)) || (R == ((8 * pattern) + 8)));
    mostPreciseBound((R < pattern) || (R == pattern));
    if (((pattern < 0) || (pattern == 0)) || ((stopIndex < pattern) || (stopIndex == pattern)))
    {
      return;
    }
    else
    {
      ;
    }
    int appendTo = 0;
    int pos = ndInt2(0, pattern - 1);
    int start = pos;
    int lastHold = start;
    int choice = 0;
    int i = pos;
    while (i < pattern)
    {
      {
        temporaryStopIndex = ndInt2(lastIndexOfStopIndex, stopIndex);
        choice = temporaryStopIndex - lastIndexOfStopIndex;
        lastIndexOfStopIndex = temporaryStopIndex;
      }
      if ((choice < 10) || (choice == 10))
      {
        pos = pos + 1;
        appendTo = appendTo + (pos - lastHold);
        D0p = D0; D0 = 0; C0 = C0 + 1;D0 = D0 + (pos - lastHold);
        R = R + (pos - lastHold);
        break;
      }
      else
      {
        ;
      }
      pos = pos + 1;
      i = i + 1;
    }
  }

abstract class GetCanonicalName  {
  void execute(int className)
  {
    int C0 = 0;
    int D0 = 0;
    int D0p = 0;
    int BOOLEAN_SEPARATOR = 10;
    int R = 0;
    lessPreciseBound((R < ((8 * className) + 8)) || (R == ((8 * className) + 8)));
    mostPreciseBound((R < className) || (R == className));
    if ((className < 0) || (className == 0))
    {
      return;
    }
    else
    {
      ;
    }
    int i = 0;

abstract class Replace  {
  void execute(int replacement, int text, int searchString, int max)
  {
    int C0 = 0;
    int C1 = 0;
    int D0 = 0;
    int D0p = 0;
    int D1 = 0;
    int D1p = 0;
    int BOOLEAN_SEPARATOR = 10;
    int R = 0;
    int temporaryText = 0;
    int lastIndexOfText = 0;
    lessPreciseBound((R < ((8 + (8 * text)) + ((8 * text) * replacement))) || (R == ((8 + (8 * text)) + ((8 * text) * replacement))));
    mostPreciseBound((R < (text + (text * replacement))) || (R == (text + (text * replacement))));
    if (((((text < 1) || (text == 1)) || ((searchString < 0) || (searchString == 0))) || ((max < 0) || (max == 0))) || ((replacement < 0) || (replacement == 0)))
    {
      return;
    }
    else
    {
      ;
    }
    int chunk = 0;
    int i = 0;
    while ((i + 1) < text)
    {
      {
        temporaryText = ndInt2(lastIndexOfText, text);
        chunk = temporaryText - lastIndexOfText;
        lastIndexOfText = temporaryText;
      }
      D0p = D0; D0 = 0; C0 = C0 + 1;D0 = D0 + chunk;
      R = R + chunk;
      D1p = D1; D1 = 0; C1 = C1 + 1;D1 = D1 + replacement;
      R = R + replacement;
      {
        temporaryText = ndInt2(lastIndexOfText, text);
        chunk = temporaryText - lastIndexOfText;
        lastIndexOfText = temporaryText;
      }
      i = i + 2;
    }
  }

                lastMatch = false;
              }
              else

              }
              sizePlus1 = sizePlus1 + 1;

            }

            }

          }
          else

            ;
          }
          lastMatch = false;
          match = true;
          i = i + 1;
        }
      }
      else
      {
        while (i < str)
        {
          if (choice < i)
          {
            if (match || preserveAllTokens)
            {
              lastMatch = true;
              if (sizePlus1 == max)
              {
                i = str;
                lastMatch = false;
              }
              else
              {

              }
              sizePlus1 = sizePlus1 + 1;

            continue;
          }
          else
          {
            ;
          }
          lastMatch = false;
          match = true;
          i = i + 1;
        }
      }
    }

    {
      list = list + (i - start);
      D1p = D1; D1 = 0; C1 = C1 + 1;D1 = D1 + (i - start);
      R = R + (i - start);
    }
    else
    {
      ;
    }
  }
